    HTTP Request

    DELETE /api/admin/customers/{customer}

    设置默认的收货地址

    Example request:

    curl -X POST \

    HTTP Request

    GET /api/admin/continents/{code?}

    获取基础配置

    Example request:

    curl -X GET \
    -G "http://wshop.docker/api/admin/options" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJhdWQiOiIyIiwianRpIjoiZTgzZDJhMzhlZjdkNWYwODFjMGE1YjExYjVmNWRiY2UwMTdiYTQ0MjE0ZThlZWMxOTgzZTFkZWQxZjViYjE0M2JmNWQ2MjRmYzYwZGMyYWEiLCJpYXQiOjE1NzkxNTc5MTMsIm5iZiI6MTU3OTE1NzkxMywiZXhwIjoxNjEwNzgwMzEzLCJzdWIiOiIyMiIsInNjb3BlcyI6WyIqIl19.rLafIlJmF5IcJrKiU8CaT0lLOLP5oOZuOUl8VN3dBA8gRR964DRd7vmioRniQAGPM4_7LqblJvmETo0DAGBe9AOWViI8I0GrMHuRMRtU-W7tRlYSIJYjwYmBeTn6IZR5QMzsLp3x86g0YSiHcEh0g37Q-hlAoIkcoxBGs0wRHusZLS3gRLpEmH5WT0ivJxDTZuRVsGz_C8a1oOv9Fqdo9Eiq3nknfbBuSXNuYG8_nE-TJ7Oxt2bHM4NCEHYV4wH90IyuqZYmm6HA0zyo34JfBrP_aVak_52qr2xo49AOZNmAMqL0oMcnjgT5vLlQSqHG-mfomPb3TnHtVWtWC0UyiQe8AQzxE7f235QR4u8_j5ozix7Pv9ZeB5maYMH3nAFMt3lYiaINGwx5q-hLEbBvLLqQHJQqt0g4JcaU5u-qvUUArOTRLrQZyZPuPC7IO9Cv2wJNMrmXrBCy_zMB_0ZrK08tpSPIRUO-CcF9zhoxBaRcVBdGCz6qsw7G0IhrahhQCxwJFWPdpparoJjdg3Rv_1okf17KU7XUqAaWSuDPFJtHl9T90lxwgX15EypeP8UCbMtN37nybyFWU6IjqsaSnoZ8oRfhH2rQM9waIQ1uKfS10lAplpQSst4JXcf4bZ7t7qNKPr-y5aie0tsCFqz2dA91HTY9FiyC6kSnq47Z4DI"

    HTTP Request

    GET /api/admin/options

    设置基础配置

    Example request:

    curl -X POST \
    "http://wshop.docker/api/admin/options" \

    HTTP Request

    POST /api/admin/orders/{id}/status

    修改发货状态

    Example request:

    curl -X POST \

    HTTP Request

    DELETE /api/admin/pages/{page}

    Product Categories

    获取产品分类

    产品分类允许一次性取出所有记录，也支持分页获取

    Example request:

    curl -X GET \
    -G "http://wshop.docker/api/admin/categories" \

    HTTP Request

    GET /api/admin/categories

    创建分类

    Example request:

    curl -X POST \
    "http://wshop.docker/api/admin/categories" \

    HTTP Request

    GET /api/admin/products

    Query Parameters

    Parameter Status Description
    filter[search] optional 搜索SKU或者产品名
    filter[category] optional 根据分类过滤,多个分类用逗号隔开
    filter[tag] optional 根据标签过滤，多个标签用逗号隔开
    filter[status] optional 获取状态过滤，允许的值, published和private
    filter optional array 所有的过滤都通过filter数组完成，支持的过滤项见其他参数说明
    sort optional 排序，目前支持date，正向排序sort=date,反向sort=-date
    includes optional 获取额外字段，默认不返回图库和变种，可以通过gallery和variants获取，多个字段用逗号隔开，例：includes=gallery,variants
    page optional 页码，从1开始
    page_size optional 每页数量，默认25

    Create Product

    创建商品是Admin中比较复杂的一个操作，分为创建简单商品和变种商品。

    创建变种商品示例

    curl -X POST \
  http://wshop.docker/api/admin/products \
  -H 'Accept: application/json' \
  -H 'Authorization: {{authorization}}' \
  -H 'Cache-Control: no-cache' \
  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
  -H 'Postman-Token: 8d481f34-f0da-fad8-75ea-d9bbb1078b24' \
  -d '{
    "title": "测试商品12233",
    "content": "商品内容测试",
    "sale_price": 18,
    "regular_price": 20,
    "manage_stock": "yes",
    "sku":"1234567898m5",
    "stock": 200,
    "backorders": "no",
    "weight": 20,
    "post_status": "publish",
    "categories": [268],
    "tags": [47, 48],
    "gallery": [
        1488,1489
    ],
    "attrs": [
        {
            "name": "color",
            "value": ["red", "yellow", "green"]
        },
        {
            "name": "size",
            "value": ["lg", "xs", "m"]
        }
    ],
    "variants": [{
        "image": 1275,
        "sku": "123456-1",
        "sale_price": 35,
        "regular_price": 40,
        "stock": 2000,
        "weight": 10,
        "attrs": [{
            "name": "color",
            "value": "red"
        }, {
            "name": "size",
            "value": "m"
        }]
    },{
        "image": 1275,
        "sku": "123456-2",
        "sale_price": 35,
        "regular_price": 40,
        "stock": 20000,
        "attrs": [{
            "name": "color",
            "value": "yellow"
        }, {
            "name": "size",
            "value": "m"
        }]
    }]
}'

    HTTP Request

    POST /api/admin/products

    Body Parameters

    Parameter Type Status Description
    title string required 产品标题
    content string optional 产品介绍
    post_status string optional 产品状态,取值: publish或private
    regular_price required optional float 常规价格
    sale_price float optional 促销价
    sku string optional sku，不允许两个产品有相同的sku
    weight number optional 重量
    manage_stock string optional 是否管理库存，取值： 'yes'或者'no'
    stock number optional 库存数量
    backorders string optional 缺货后是否可以继续销售，取值： 'yes'或者'no'
    tags array optional 标签列表
    categories array optional 分类列表
    gallery array optional 图片列表
    attrs array optional 属性列表
    variants array optional 变种列表
    variants.*.image integer optional 缩略图
    variants.*.regular_price float optional 价格
    variants.*.sale_price float optional 促销价
    variants.*.stock integer optional 库存

    Get Product

    Example request:

    curl -X GET \
    -G "http://wshop.docker/api/admin/products/1" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJhdWQiOiIyIiwianRpIjoiZTgzZDJhMzhlZjdkNWYwODFjMGE1YjExYjVmNWRiY2UwMTdiYTQ0MjE0ZThlZWMxOTgzZTFkZWQxZjViYjE0M2JmNWQ2MjRmYzYwZGMyYWEiLCJpYXQiOjE1NzkxNTc5MTMsIm5iZiI6MTU3OTE1NzkxMywiZXhwIjoxNjEwNzgwMzEzLCJzdWIiOiIyMiIsInNjb3BlcyI6WyIqIl19.rLafIlJmF5IcJrKiU8CaT0lLOLP5oOZuOUl8VN3dBA8gRR964DRd7vmioRniQAGPM4_7LqblJvmETo0DAGBe9AOWViI8I0GrMHuRMRtU-W7tRlYSIJYjwYmBeTn6IZR5QMzsLp3x86g0YSiHcEh0g37Q-hlAoIkcoxBGs0wRHusZLS3gRLpEmH5WT0ivJxDTZuRVsGz_C8a1oOv9Fqdo9Eiq3nknfbBuSXNuYG8_nE-TJ7Oxt2bHM4NCEHYV4wH90IyuqZYmm6HA0zyo34JfBrP_aVak_52qr2xo49AOZNmAMqL0oMcnjgT5vLlQSqHG-mfomPb3TnHtVWtWC0UyiQe8AQzxE7f235QR4u8_j5ozix7Pv9ZeB5maYMH3nAFMt3lYiaINGwx5q-hLEbBvLLqQHJQqt0g4JcaU5u-qvUUArOTRLrQZyZPuPC7IO9Cv2wJNMrmXrBCy_zMB_0ZrK08tpSPIRUO-CcF9zhoxBaRcVBdGCz6qsw7G0IhrahhQCxwJFWPdpparoJjdg3Rv_1okf17KU7XUqAaWSuDPFJtHl9T90lxwgX15EypeP8UCbMtN37nybyFWU6IjqsaSnoZ8oRfhH2rQM9waIQ1uKfS10lAplpQSst4JXcf4bZ7t7qNKPr-y5aie0tsCFqz2dA91HTY9FiyC6kSnq47Z4DI"

    HTTP Request

    GET /api/admin/products/{product}

    Update Product

    Example request:

    curl -X PUT \

    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJhdWQiOiIyIiwianRpIjoiZTgzZDJhMzhlZjdkNWYwODFjMGE1YjExYjVmNWRiY2UwMTdiYTQ0MjE0ZThlZWMxOTgzZTFkZWQxZjViYjE0M2JmNWQ2MjRmYzYwZGMyYWEiLCJpYXQiOjE1NzkxNTc5MTMsIm5iZiI6MTU3OTE1NzkxMywiZXhwIjoxNjEwNzgwMzEzLCJzdWIiOiIyMiIsInNjb3BlcyI6WyIqIl19.rLafIlJmF5IcJrKiU8CaT0lLOLP5oOZuOUl8VN3dBA8gRR964DRd7vmioRniQAGPM4_7LqblJvmETo0DAGBe9AOWViI8I0GrMHuRMRtU-W7tRlYSIJYjwYmBeTn6IZR5QMzsLp3x86g0YSiHcEh0g37Q-hlAoIkcoxBGs0wRHusZLS3gRLpEmH5WT0ivJxDTZuRVsGz_C8a1oOv9Fqdo9Eiq3nknfbBuSXNuYG8_nE-TJ7Oxt2bHM4NCEHYV4wH90IyuqZYmm6HA0zyo34JfBrP_aVak_52qr2xo49AOZNmAMqL0oMcnjgT5vLlQSqHG-mfomPb3TnHtVWtWC0UyiQe8AQzxE7f235QR4u8_j5ozix7Pv9ZeB5maYMH3nAFMt3lYiaINGwx5q-hLEbBvLLqQHJQqt0g4JcaU5u-qvUUArOTRLrQZyZPuPC7IO9Cv2wJNMrmXrBCy_zMB_0ZrK08tpSPIRUO-CcF9zhoxBaRcVBdGCz6qsw7G0IhrahhQCxwJFWPdpparoJjdg3Rv_1okf17KU7XUqAaWSuDPFJtHl9T90lxwgX15EypeP8UCbMtN37nybyFWU6IjqsaSnoZ8oRfhH2rQM9waIQ1uKfS10lAplpQSst4JXcf4bZ7t7qNKPr-y5aie0tsCFqz2dA91HTY9FiyC6kSnq47Z4DI"

    HTTP Request

    PUT /api/admin/products/{product}

    PATCH /api/admin/products/{product}

    Delete Product

    如果有订单则不允许删除

    Example request:

    curl -X DELETE \
    "http://wshop.docker/api/admin/products/1" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json" \
